#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = fluxSrc

# set the receiver in the scan coordinator to avoid errors
SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# configuring manually to avoid re-tuning
Configure(point_config) # configure the pointing at the frequency of the source.
execfile(projectDir+"/addwx.py")

Slew(source)

Balance()

# pointing
AutoPeak(source,configure=False) # This peaks at the frequency of the source.

Break("enter pointing offsets")

# focusing
Focus(source) 

Break("enter focus values if necessary")

# Below is the old daisy pattern in case it's useful.

# daisy pattern -- copied from GBT Observer's Guide
# nosc=22.0
# #map_radius = 2.8 # arcminutes
# map_radius = 1.5 # arcminutes
# #radial_osc_period = 25.0 # seconds
# radial_osc_period = 28.0 # seconds
# #n_scans = 5 # split 22 oscillations over 5 scans
# n_scans = 4 # split 22 oscillations over 4 scans
# daisyScanDuration = nosc * radial_osc_period / n_scans
# phi2 = 2.0 * nosc /n_scans
# phi1 = 3.14159265 * phi2
# # Note -- increment rotation_phase by phi2 each scans
# #         -- increment radial_phase by phi1 each scan

# print daisyScanDuration

# for i in range(n_scans):
#     Daisy(source,map_radius,radial_osc_period,i*phi1,i*phi2,
#                 daisyScanDuration, beamName='10',coordMode='J2000',
#                 cos_v=True,calc_dt=0.2)

# Below is the old daisy pattern in case it's useful.

# daisy pattern -- copied from GBT Observer's Guide
# nosc=22.0
# #map_radius = 2.8 # arcminutes
# map_radius = 1.5 # arcminutes
# #radial_osc_period = 25.0 # seconds
# radial_osc_period = 28.0 # seconds
# #n_scans = 5 # split 22 oscillations over 5 scans
# n_scans = 4 # split 22 oscillations over 4 scans
# daisyScanDuration = nosc * radial_osc_period / n_scans
# phi2 = 2.0 * nosc /n_scans
# phi1 = 3.14159265 * phi2
# # Note -- increment rotation_phase by phi2 each scans
# #         -- increment radial_phase by phi1 each scan

# print daisyScanDuration

# for i in range(n_scans):
#     Daisy(source,map_radius,radial_osc_period,i*phi1,i*phi2,
#                 daisyScanDuration, beamName='10',coordMode='J2000',
#                 cos_v=True,calc_dt=0.2)

execfile(projectDir+"/addwx.py")

Slew(galaxyName)
Balance()

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

RALongMap( galaxyName,
           Offset("J2000", mymap['scanLength']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0,  mymap['mapHeight']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['step']/3600., cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # can add start and stop row parameters to the above, 
	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

#load catalogs

source = pointSrc

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

print "Integration time per row (s): ", mymap['scanDuration']
print "Offset between map rows (arcsec): ", mymap['step']
print "Length of scan (arcmin): ", mymap['scanLength']
print "Height of map (arcmin): ",  mymap['mapHeight']

Configure(argus_config)
execfile(projectDir+"/addwx.py")

Slew(galaxyName)
Balance()

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

RALongMap( galaxyName,
           Offset("J2000", mymap['scanLength']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0,  mymap['mapHeight']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['step']/3600., cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # can add start and stop row parameters to the above, 
	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

#load catalogs

## may want to set LO frequency here

Focus(source) 

Break("enter focus values if necessary")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig()
